Standard Showdown Decks, Week 2
===============================



 Posted in **Feature**
 on December 9, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_BlakeRasmussen.jpg)
By Blake Rasmussen




Blake is the content manager for DailyMTG.com, making him the one you should email if you have thoughts on the website, good or less good (or not good). He's a longtime coverage reporter and hasn't turned down a game of Magic in any format ever. 






The third round of Standard Showdown events is this weekend, but if you need inspiration for what to play, we'll be publishing decks from the previous weekend every Friday. If you want to just see deck lists, scroll down.


I received a lot of cool decks (you can email [standardshowdown@wizards.com](mailto:standardshowdown@wizards.com) to see your deck here next week), but I also received a lot of cool notes from players and stores just saying how much fun the event was. Here's just a few things people wrote while sending in their decklists:




---

As a new player (started in October because *Kaladesh* looked great) I play Standard by necessity, and so the Standard Showdown looked like a lot of fun. It was! As a break from exam studies, I decided last minute to attend and took a homebrew I'd made for fun the night before. Somehow it took me to 4-0 for my first tournament win!


The Showdown was so much fun, and as a very new player I am excited to see this sort of event. I look forward to seeing what's next!




---

Some of the closest games of *Magic* I've had in a while. Especially the third game of the final round. Almost died to [Marionette Master](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Marionette+Master), but I just managed to squeeze out enough trample damage to pull off the win. (Thank you [Neck Breaker](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Neck+Breaker), [Cult](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?multiverseid=409959), [Alphas](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?multiverseid=414414), and others. But mostly [Neck Breaker](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Neck+Breaker).)




---

This deck has [helped] me go undefeated twice. Feels so good to have your opponent tap out when you have Bruna coming out next turn and Brisela makes their hand full of blanks.




---

Standard Showdown has been well-received in my local game store. New faces, lots of different decks, and great atmosphere. And not to mention the excitement of opening the Standard Showdown boosters!




---

I would say this is the best promotion Wizards had ever made, and you should think about doing something similar next year during this time. Also, this is the best experience I've had in around 20 years of *Magic*, and I would say thanks to all of Wizards of the Coast!




---

Love Standard Showdown. Keep doing it after the four weeks.




---

I really enjoyed the Showdown. This gave the whole event a more casual feel. I won two special packs, and the premium foil full-art Mountain went right into my deck.




---

**4-0**

Standard Showdown is four-week event celebrating all that is Standard, with local tournaments, cool prizes, and opportunities for bragging rights and brewing.


Looking for a Standard Showdown tournament near you? Use this locator to find your nearest store hosting one of these fun events.

Already been to an event and crushed it? Submit your name, decklist, record, store where you played, and any fun photos you have at [standardshowdown@wizards.com](mailto:standardshowdown@wizards.com) or by filling out the form below.
